</td></tr><tr><td><b>eIndicatorType</b></td><td><code>3</code></td></tr><tr><td><b>unk_9c1ea4f</b></td><td><code>0</code></td></tr><tr><td><b>szOnCallbackCompleteScript</b></td><td><pre>function Start()
	
	-- Setup camel to follow Meshif
	Hydra.ActorClearAnimSetOverride(LORATH_STORM)
	Hydra.Wait(1)

	-- workaround for npcs not moving
	Hydra.ActorClearAnimSetOverride(MESHIF_INTRO)
	Hydra.QActorEnableAI(MESHIFCAMEL_INTRO, false)
	Hydra.QActorStopAllQueuedActions(MESHIFCAMEL_INTRO)
	Hydra.QActorStopAllQueuedActions(MESHIF_INTRO)
	
	-- set starting paths and attach rope from meshif to camel
	Hydra.ActorPlayEffectGroupActorToActor(MESHIF_INTRO, MESHIFCAMEL_INTRO, "NPC_Camel_guide", true)
	Hydra.Wait(2)
	Hydra.ActorSetNodePath(MESHIF_INTRO, ESCORT_PATH_01, Hydra.PATH_FOLLOW_ONE_WAY, false)
	-- set the camel to follow meshif
	Hydra.QActorFollowPathDynamicSpeed(MESHIF_INTRO, ESCORT_PATH_01, "NPC_Run_Slow", false)

	Hydra.Wait(1)
	Hydra.ActorSetFollowTarget(MESHIFCAMEL_INTRO, MESHIF_INTRO, Hydra.FOLLOW_TYPE_DEFAULT);
	Hydra.QActorFadeAndDelete(MESHIF_INTRO, 1.0)
	Hydra.WaitForQEmpty(MESHIF_INTRO)
	Hydra.QActorFadeAndDelete(MESHIFCAMEL_INTRO, 1.0)
	Hydra.ActorEnable(MESHIF_TREK)
	Hydra.ActorEnable(MESHIFCAMEL_TREK)

end
</pre></td></tr><tr><td><b>fDebugDisable</b></td><td><code>0</code></td></tr><tr><td><b>arSubzones</b></td><td></td></tr><tr><td><b>arRegionOverrides</b></td><td></td></tr><tr><td><b>arSnonameTokens</b></td><td></td></tr><tr><td><b>unk_5342cc0</b></td><td><code>0</code></td></tr><tr><td><b>tScriptMessageMap</b></td><td><table><tr><th colspan="100%">ScriptMessageMap</th></tr><tr><td><b>dwListenerFlags</b></td><td><code>0</code></td></tr><tr><td><b>unk_c3ba01d</b></td><td><code>0</code></td></tr><tr><td><b>flCooldownSeconds</b></td><td><code>0</code></td></tr><tr><td><b>arEventFilters</b></td><td></td></tr><tr><td><b>unk_492729e</b></td><td></td></tr><tr><td><b>unk_9927fd3</b></td><td><code>58</code></td></tr><tr><td><b>eEventType</b></td><td><code>65</code></td></tr></table>

	-- run meshif to safe zone 2. camel moves to position when meshif reaches the safe zone
	Hydra.QActorStopAllQueuedActions(MESHIF_TREK)
	---Disable Meshif's AI to prevent path looping
	Hydra.ActorDisableAI(MESHIF_TREK)
	Hydra.ActorDisableAI(MESHIFCAMEL_TREK)
	
	Hydra.Wait(0.5)
	--Move Meshif and Camel to safezone location
	Hydra.QActorMoveToLocationDynamicSpeed(MESHIF_TREK, MARKER_SANDSTORM_SAFE_02, "NPC_Walk_Fast", true)
	Hydra.QActorMoveToLocationDynamicSpeed(MESHIFCAMEL_TREK, CAMEL_SANDSTORM_SAFE_02, "NPC_Walk_Fast", true)
	Hydra.QActorFaceSameAsActor(MESHIFCAMEL_TREK, CAMEL_SANDSTORM_SAFE_02)
	Hydra.QActorClearAnimSetOverride(MESHIF_TREK)
	Hydra.QActorFaceSameAsActor(MESHIF_TREK, MARKER_SANDSTORM_SAFE_02)
	Hydra.Wait(1.0)
	Hydra.ActorSetAnimSetOverride(MESHIF_TREK, S_SANDSTORM_ANIMSET)
	
	-- have lorath run for cover
	idLorathFollower = Hydra.QuestGetFollower("NPC_QST_Lorath_Follower")
	
	if Hydra.ActorIsValid(idLorathFollower) then
		Hydra.QuestFollowerTakeOwnership(idLorathFollower)
		Hydra.QActorMoveToLocationDynamicSpeed(idLorathFollower, LORATH_SANDSTORM_SAFE_02, "NPC_Walk_Fast", true)
		Hydra.QActorFaceSameAsActor(idLorathFollower, LORATH_SANDSTORM_SAFE_02)
	end

end

	if Hydra.ActorIsValid(idLorathFollower) then
		Hydra.QActorStopAllQueuedActions(idLorathFollower)
	end	
	
	Hydra.QActorStopAllQueuedActions(MESHIF_TREK)
	Hydra.QActorMoveToLocationDynamicSpeed(MESHIF_TREK, MARKER_SANDSTORM_SAFE_04, "NPC_Walk_Fast", true)
	Hydra.QActorClearAnimSetOverride(MESHIF_TREK)
	Hydra.QActorFaceSameAsActor(MESHIF_TREK, MARKER_SANDSTORM_SAFE_04)
	
	Hydra.Wait(1)

	-- have lorath run for cover
	idLorathFollower = Hydra.QuestGetFollower("NPC_QST_Lorath_Follower")
	
	if Hydra.ActorIsValid(idLorathFollower) then
		Hydra.QuestFollowerTakeOwnership(idLorathFollower)
		Hydra.QActorMoveToLocationDynamicSpeed(idLorathFollower, LORATH_SANDSTORM_SAFE_04, "NPC_Walk_Fast", true)
		Hydra.QActorFaceSameAsActor(idLorathFollower, LORATH_SANDSTORM_SAFE_04)
	end
	-- set the animset override for the storm
	Hydra.ActorSetAnimSetOverride(MESHIF_TREK, S_SANDSTORM_ANIMSET)
end
